						AND BSubS.LEFT_MARGIN>=BS.LEFT_MARGIN
						AND BSubS.RIGHT_MARGIN<=BS.RIGHT_MARGIN)

					) BES ON BES.IBLOCK_ELEMENT_ID = BE.ID

						AND (((SITE_ID='s1')))
					))

			)

				WHERE ER.ELEMENT_ID = BE.ID
